    function() {
      var $ = jQuery;
      var buyBoxGrid = $('table.buyingDetailsGrid');
      var setFallback = function(dpState) {

        if (dpState) {
          if (dpState.current_asin) {
            $('.wishlistAddButtonActive, .wishlistDownButtonActive', buyBoxGrid).show();
            $('.wishlistAddButtonInactive, .wishlistDownButtonInactive', buyBoxGrid).hide();
          } else {
            $('.wishlistAddButtonActive, .wishlistDownButtonActive', buyBoxGrid).hide();
            $('.wishlistAddButtonInactive, .wishlistDownButtonInactive', buyBoxGrid).show();
          }
        }
        var fixupDelay = 100;
        var fixupFunc = function() {
          fixupDelay *= 2;
          if (fixupDelay < 10000) {
            setTimeout(fixupFunc, fixupDelay);
          }
        };
        setTimeout(fixupFunc, fixupDelay);
      };

      var hookFunc;
      var count = 0;
      hookFunc = function() {
        if (typeof DetailPageFramework != 'undefined' && DetailPageFramework.registerCallback) {
          DetailPageFramework.registerFeatureConfig('wishlist', { dataType: 'atf', priority: 'high', suppressDefaultBehavior: true});
          DetailPageFramework.registerCallback('asin_select', 'wishlist', setFallback);
          DetailPageFramework.registerCallback('asin_deselect', 'wishlist', setFallback);
        } else {
          if (count++ < 20) {
            setTimeout(hookFunc, 1000);
          }
        }
      };
      hookFunc();
      setFallback();
    });
   }
}

    <script type="text/javascript">
        window.SizingChart = function() {
            var isOpen = false;
            var open = function(link) {
                amznJQ.available("jQuery", function() {
                    var spinnerContent = "<div id='size-chart-spinner'><img src='"
                        + window.AmazonPopoverImages.snake + "'/></div>";
                    var url = jQuery(link).attr("href");
                    if (window.gOpenQuickview) {
                        window.gOpenQuickview.showSizingChart(url);
                    } else {
                        if(isOpen) return;
                        isOpen = true;
                        amznJQ.available("popover", function() {
                            var popover =  jQuery.AmazonPopover.displayPopover({
                                    literalContent: spinnerContent,
                                    location:"centered",
                                    width:800,
                                    zIndex:991,
                                    height:height,
                                    locationOffset:[0, -50],
                                    title:"尺码对照表",
                                    closeText:"关闭",
                                    onHide: function() {
                                        isOpen = false;
                                    }
                                });

                            var iframeHeight = jQuery(window).height() - 180;
                            var height = Math.min(Math.max(iframeHeight,300), 700);

                            var fetchAjax = function() {
                                jQuery.ajax({
                                    url:url+"&height="+height,
                                    success: function(data) {
                                        data = data.replace(/\s*([^\s]*)\s*$/, "$1");
                                        if(data) {
                                            popover.find(".ap_content").html(data);
                                        } else {
                                            ajaxFailure();
                                        }
                                    },
                                    error: function() {
                                        ajaxFailure();
                                    }
                                });
                            };

                            var ajaxFailure = function() {
                                popover.find(".ap_content").html("<div id='size-chart-error'><p class='error-text'>对不起，由于暂时行原因，目前尺码对照表无法显示。</p><p><a href='" + url + "'>请再试一遍</a></p></div>");

                                popover.find("#size-chart-error a").click(function() {
                                    popover.find(".ap_content").html(spinnerContent);
                                    fetchAjax();
                                    return false;
                                });
                            };

                            fetchAjax();
                        });
                    }
                });

                return false;
            };

            return { open : open };
        }();
    </script>

<script type="text/javascript">


  function ajaxUpdate(stateIdx,cityIdx,districtIdx,ASIN,updateSembu,addressSelectSource){

    var params = [];
    params.push("stateIndex=" + encodeURIComponent(stateIdx));
    params.push("cityIndex=" + encodeURIComponent(cityIdx));
    params.push("districtIndex=" + encodeURIComponent(districtIdx));
    params.push("ASIN=" + ASIN);
    params.push("rd=" + Math.random());
    params.push("token=" + encodeURIComponent(jQuery("#ddmToken").text()));
    params.push("updateSembu=" + updateSembu);
    params.push("addressSelectSource=" + addressSelectSource);
    
    jQuery.ajax({
      type: "POST",
      url: "/gp/product/features/dynamic-delivery-message/generate-dynamic-delivery-message.html?ie=UTF8&ie=UTF8",
      contentType: 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded;charset=utf-8',
      data: params.join('&'),
      dataType: "html",
      success: function(objResponse) {
        var resp = objResponse;
        jQuery("#ddmDynamicDisplay").html(resp);
      },
      error: function(xhr) {
        jQuery("#ddmDynamicDisplay").html("对不起，服务器正忙，请稍后再查看配送时间。 ");
      }
    }); // end of jQuery.ajax()
  }
</script>

            closeEventInclude: "CLICK_OUTSIDE",
            onHide: function(popover){
              jQuery("#ddm-shipto-click").hide();
            },
            onShow: function(popover){
                jQuery("#ddm-destination-address").height(34) ;
                var visibleStrLen = 0;
                jQuery("#ddm-destination-address span").each(function(){
                    if (jQuery(this).css("display") != "none") {
                        visibleStrLen += jQuery(this).text().length;
                    }
                });
                visibleStrLen = (visibleStrLen == 0) ? 20 : visibleStrLen;
                var popoverZindex = popover.css("z-index");
                jQuery("#ddm-shipto-click").css("position","absolute").css("width",visibleStrLen * 12 + 75).css("top",jQuery("#ddmPopoverArea-left").offset().top-5).css("left",jQuery("#ddmPopoverArea-left").offset().left).css("z-index",popoverZindex).show();
              if( popover != null){
                  ddmPopover = popover;
                  if( ddmSelection.selectedState == "" &&  jQuery("#ddmDeliveryToState").html() != null){
                      ddmSelection.selectedState = jQuery("#ddmDeliveryToState").html();
                      ddmSelection.selectedCity = jQuery("#ddmDeliveryToCity").html();
                      ddmSelection.selectedDistrict = jQuery("#ddmDeliveryToDistrict").html();
                  }
                  
                  var strLength = 0;
                  var stateTriggerText = jQuery("#stateTrigger").text();
                  var cityTriggerText = jQuery("#cityTrigger").text();
                  var districtTriggerText = jQuery("#districtTrigger").text();
                  if (stateTriggerText != null && stateTriggerText != ""){
                      strLength += stateTriggerText.length;
                  } else {
                      strLength += 4;
                  }
                  if (cityTriggerText != null && cityTriggerText != ""){
                      strLength += cityTriggerText.length;
                  } else {
                      strLength += 5;
                  }
                  if (districtTriggerText != null && districtTriggerText != ""){
                      strLength += districtTriggerText.length;
                  } else {
                      strLength += 5;
                  }
                  
                  var stateCityDistrictLineWidth = 252 + strLength * 12;
        
                  var customerAddressLineWidth = 0;
                      var listMaxStrLength = 0;
                      jQuery("#ddm_customer_address_list a").each(function(){
                          var tmpListTextLength = jQuery(this).text().length;
                          if (listMaxStrLength < tmpListTextLength) {
                              listMaxStrLength = tmpListTextLength;
                          }
                      });
                      customerAddressLineWidth = 120 + listMaxStrLength * 12;

    
                  if (customerAddressLineWidth > stateCityDistrictLineWidth) {
                      ddmPopover.width(customerAddressLineWidth);    
                  } else {
                      ddmPopover.width(stateCityDistrictLineWidth);
                  }
        
                  ddmPopover.click(function(){
                      var popoverZindex = popover.css("z-index");
                      jQuery("#ddm-shipto-click").css("z-index",popoverZindex);
                  });
              }
           }
        });
     });

        ddmCountDown.getLeftTimeString = function ( remainSeconds ) {
          if (remainSeconds <= 0) return undefined; 
          var remainMins = Math.floor(remainSeconds / 60);
          var minutes = remainMins % 60;
          var hours = Math.floor(remainMins / 60);
          var seconds = remainSeconds % 60;
          var inNext = "内";
          var hourString   =  ( hours == 1 ? "小时" : "小时" );
          var minuteString =  ( minutes  == 1 ? "分钟" : "分钟" );
          var secondString =  ( seconds  == 1 ? "秒" : "秒" );
          if ( hours > 0 && minutes > 0 ){
            return hours + hourString + minutes + minuteString + inNext;
          } else if( hours > 0 && minutes == 0 ){
            return hours + hourString + inNext;
          } else if( hours == 0 && minutes > 0 ){
            return minutes + minuteString + inNext;
          } else if( hours == 0 && minutes == 0 ){
            return seconds + secondString + inNext;
          }

amznJQ.onCompletion('amznJQ.criticalFeature', function() {
  amznJQ.available('search-js-jq', function(){});
  amznJQ.available('amazonShoveler', function(){});
  amznJQ.available('simsJS', function(){});
  amznJQ.available('cmuAnnotations', function(){});

  amznJQ.available('amzn-ratings-bar', function(){});
  amznJQ.available('accessoriesJS', function(){});
  amznJQ.available('priceformatterJS', function(){});
  amznJQ.available('CustomerPopover', function(){});

if (!window.DPClientLogger) {
    window.DPClientLogger = {};
}

window.DPClientLogger.ImpressionLogger = function( program_group, feature, forceUpload) {
    var self = this,
    data = {};

    self.logImpression = function(key) {
      data[key]=1;
      setTimeout( self.upload, 2000 ); // upload client side metrics after 2secs of recording it.  
    };

    self.upload = function() {
      var t = [];
      jQuery.each(data, function(k,v){ t.push(k); });
      data = {};
      if(t.length > 0){
        var protocol = location.protocol == "https:" ? "https://" : "http://",
            url = protocol + ue.furl + "/1/action-impressions/1/OP/" + program_group + "/action/" + feature + ":" + t.join() + "?marketplaceId=" + ue.mid + "&requestId=" + ue.rid + "&session=" + ue.sid + "&_=" + (new Date()).getTime();
        (new Image()).src = url;
      }
    };

    if(forceUpload) {
        jQuery(window).unload(function() { self.upload();});
    }
};
amznJQ.onReady("jQuery", function(){
  amznJQ.declareAvailable("DPClientLogger");
});

});
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
var ma_doc;
var DPCL;

var ma_clicked = 0;
var ma_lastCheck = 0; // timestamp to prevent us messing with the DOM too often
var ma_initCP = 0; // init check pending flag to prevent queueing up of multiple event handler calls
var topCalculatedForNONIE = 0;

var showHideMiniATF = function(isResizeEvent) {
  // Haven't serviced last one yet!
  if(ma_initCP && !isResizeEvent) { return ; }

  // Don't look at the DOM more than once every 400ms
  var lastCheckDiff = new Date().getTime() - ma_lastCheck;
  var checkDelay = (lastCheckDiff < 100 ? 100 - lastCheckDiff : 10);

  ma_initCP = 1;        
  
  var initIfNeeded = function() {
      // show miniATF if Y offset is > 850px else hide it, and show/hide with 200ms delay
      var yPos = ma_doc.scrollTop(), miniATF = jQuery("#gTTLink");
      if( yPos > 650 ){
        
          if( !ma_clicked && miniATF.is(':hidden')){
             miniATF.slideDown(200);
        }
      } else {
        if(miniATF.is(':visible')) 
          miniATF.slideUp(200);
        ma_clicked=0;
      }

      ma_initCP = 0;
      ma_lastCheck = new Date().getTime();
  };

  // Call this function outside of the scroll handler to avoid slowing down scrolling
  setTimeout(initIfNeeded, checkDelay);
};
if(amznJQ) 
 amznJQ.onCompletion('amznJQ.criticalFeature', function() {
  amznJQ.onReady("jQuery", function() {
    ma_doc = jQuery(window);
    jQuery("#gTTLink .ma-back-img").addClass("nav-sprite");
    ma_doc.scroll(function(){showHideMiniATF(0);});
    ma_doc.resize(function(){showHideMiniATF(1);});
    var nonHoverState = function(){
      jQuery("#gTTLink .ma-title").css("color", "#333");
    };
    // go to top on clicking on title with 300ms of scrolling behavior
    jQuery("#gTTLink .maplink, #gTTLink .ma_seeall, #gTTLink .goto-top, #gTTLink .see-all-buying-options").click(function(){ 
      ma_clicked=1;

      if( jQuery(this).hasClass("maplink")){ jQuery(this).attr("href", "javascript:void(0);"); }

      jQuery("#gTTLink").slideUp();
      jQuery("body,html").animate({scrollTop: 0}, 300); 
      nonHoverState();
      return false;
       
    });

    jQuery("#gTTLink .can-add-to-cart").click(function(){ jQuery("#gTTLink .can-add-to-cart a").children().click() } );
    
    // setup on hover experience
    jQuery("#gTTLink .ma-title").hover(function(){ 
      jQuery("#gTTLink .ma-title").css("color", "#E47911");
    }, nonHoverState );
  });
 });
</script>
</div>

</div>

amznJQ.onReady('JQuery', function() { (function($) {

    window.RECS_rhfShvlLoading = false;
    window.RECS_rhfShvlLoaded = false;
    window.RECS_rhfInView = false;
    window.RECS_rhfMetrics = {};
    $("#rhf_container").show();
    var rhfShvlEventHandler = function () {
        if (   ! window.RECS_rhfShvlLoaded
            && ! window.RECS_rhfShvlLoading
            && $('#rhf_container').size() > 0 ) {
            var yPosition = $(window).scrollTop() + $(window).height();
            var rhfElementFound = $('#rhfMainHeading').size();
            var rhfPosition = $('#rhfMainHeading').offset().top;

            if (/webkit.*mobile/i.test(navigator.userAgent)) {
                rhfPosition -= $(window).scrollTop();
            }

            if (rhfElementFound && ( rhfPosition - yPosition < 400 )) {
                window.RECS_rhfMetrics["start"] = (new Date()).getTime();
                window.RECS_rhfShvlLoading = true;
                var handleSuccess = function (html) {
                    $("#rhf_container").html(html);
                    $("#rhf0Shvl").trigger("render-shoveler");
                    window.RECS_rhfShvlLoaded = true;
                    window.RECS_rhfMetrics["loaded"] = (new Date()).getTime();
                };
                var handleError = function () {
                    $("#rhf_container").hide();
                    $("#rhf_error").show();
                    window.RECS_rhfMetrics["loaded"] = "error";
                };
                $.ajax({
                    url: '/gp/history/external/full-rhf-rec-handler.html',
                    type: "POST",
                    timeout: 10000,
                    data: {
                        shovelerName    : 'rhf0',
                        key             : 'rhf',
                        numToPreload    : '8',
                        isGateway       : 0,
                        refTag          : 'pd_rhf_dp',
                        parentSession   : '479-7800970-2826263',

                        renderPopover   : 0,

                        currentSubPageType : 'Glance',
                        searchAlias     : "",
                        keywords        : "",
                        node            : ""
                    },
                    dataType: "html",
                    success: function (data, status) {
                        handleSuccess(data);
                    },
                    error: function (xhr, status) {
                        handleError();
                    }
                });
            }
        }
    };
    var rhfInView = function() {
        if (!window.RECS_rhfInView && $('#rhf_container').size() > 0) {
            var yPosition = $(window).scrollTop() + $(window).height();
            var rhfElementFound = ($('#rhfMainHeading').size() > 0);
            var rhfPosition = $('#rhfMainHeading').offset().top;
            if (/webkit.*mobile/i.test(navigator.userAgent)) {
                rhfPosition -= $(window).scrollTop();

            if (rhfElementFound && ( rhfPosition - yPosition < 0 )) {
                window.RECS_rhfInView = true;
                window.RECS_rhfMetrics["inView"] = (new Date()).getTime();
            }
        }
    };
    $(document).ready(rhfShvlEventHandler);
    $(window).scroll(rhfShvlEventHandler);
    $(document).ready(rhfInView);
    $(window).scroll(rhfInView);

    function() {
      var $ = jQuery;
      var buyBoxGrid = $('table.buyingDetailsGrid');
      var setFallback = function(dpState) {

        if (dpState) {
          if (dpState.current_asin) {
            $('.wishlistAddButtonActive, .wishlistDownButtonActive', buyBoxGrid).show();
            $('.wishlistAddButtonInactive, .wishlistDownButtonInactive', buyBoxGrid).hide();
          } else {
            $('.wishlistAddButtonActive, .wishlistDownButtonActive', buyBoxGrid).hide();
            $('.wishlistAddButtonInactive, .wishlistDownButtonInactive', buyBoxGrid).show();
          }
        }
        var fixupDelay = 100;
        var fixupFunc = function() {
          fixupDelay *= 2;
          if (fixupDelay < 10000) {
            setTimeout(fixupFunc, fixupDelay);
          }
        };
        setTimeout(fixupFunc, fixupDelay);
      };

      var hookFunc;
      var count = 0;
      hookFunc = function() {
        if (typeof DetailPageFramework != 'undefined' && DetailPageFramework.registerCallback) {
          DetailPageFramework.registerFeatureConfig('wishlist', { dataType: 'atf', priority: 'high', suppressDefaultBehavior: true});
          DetailPageFramework.registerCallback('asin_select', 'wishlist', setFallback);
          DetailPageFramework.registerCallback('asin_deselect', 'wishlist', setFallback);
        } else {
          if (count++ < 20) {
            setTimeout(hookFunc, 1000);
          }
        }
      };
      hookFunc();
      setFallback();
    });
   }
}

  var w = window.innerWidth || document.body.offsetWidth;

  var widths = [1280,1440,1640,1800];
  var stretchyImageSizes = [[342,445],[385,500],[425,550],[466,606],[506,658]];

  var sz = 0;
  for(; sz < widths.length && w >= widths[sz]; sz++);
  
  var miw = document.getElementById("image-block-widget");
  miw.className = miw.className.replace(/size[0-9]+/,"size"+sz);

  var mi = document.getElementById("original-main-image");
  var landingImgURL = mi.src;
  if (landingImgURL && landingImgURL.match(/_SY\d+_/)) {
    mi.height = stretchyImageSizes[sz][1];
  } else {
    mi.width = stretchyImageSizes[sz][0];
  }

  var stretchyImages = ["http://ec4.images-amazon.com/images/I/81PcFLS3CAL._SX342_SY445_CR,0,0,342,445_.jpg","http://ec4.images-amazon.com/images/I/81PcFLS3CAL._SX385_SY500_CR,0,0,385,500_.jpg","http://ec4.images-amazon.com/images/I/81PcFLS3CAL._SX425_SY550_CR,0,0,425,550_.jpg","http://ec4.images-amazon.com/images/I/81PcFLS3CAL._SX466_SY606_CR,0,0,466,606_.jpg","http://ec4.images-amazon.com/images/I/81PcFLS3CAL._SX506_SY658_CR,0,0,506,658_.jpg"];
  
  amznJQ.onCompletion("amznJQ.criticalFeature", function() {
    var src = stretchyImages[sz];
    var img = new Image();
    img.onload = function() {
      var clone = mi.cloneNode(true);
      clone.src = src;
      clone.removeAttribute("width");
      clone.removeAttribute("height");
      clone.removeAttribute("onload");
      mi.parentNode.replaceChild(clone, mi);
      mi = clone;
    };
    img.src = src;
  });
  window.imageBlock.stretchyGoodnessSize = sz;
</script>

    <script type="text/javascript">
        window.SizingChart = function() {
            var isOpen = false;
            var open = function(link) {
                amznJQ.available("jQuery", function() {
                    var spinnerContent = "<div id='size-chart-spinner'><img src='"
                        + window.AmazonPopoverImages.snake + "'/></div>";
                    var url = jQuery(link).attr("href");
                    if (window.gOpenQuickview) {
                        window.gOpenQuickview.showSizingChart(url);
                    } else {
                        if(isOpen) return;
                        isOpen = true;
                        amznJQ.available("popover", function() {
                            var popover =  jQuery.AmazonPopover.displayPopover({
                                    literalContent: spinnerContent,
                                    location:"centered",
                                    width:800,
                                    zIndex:991,
                                    height:height,
                                    locationOffset:[0, -50],
                                    title:"尺码对照表",
                                    closeText:"关闭",
                                    onHide: function() {
                                        isOpen = false;
                                    }
                                });

                            var iframeHeight = jQuery(window).height() - 180;
                            var height = Math.min(Math.max(iframeHeight,300), 700);

                            var fetchAjax = function() {
                                jQuery.ajax({
                                    url:url+"&height="+height,
                                    success: function(data) {
                                        data = data.replace(/\s*([^\s]*)\s*$/, "$1");
                                        if(data) {
                                            popover.find(".ap_content").html(data);
                                        } else {
                                            ajaxFailure();
                                        }
                                    },
                                    error: function() {
                                        ajaxFailure();
                                    }
                                });
                            };

                            var ajaxFailure = function() {
                                popover.find(".ap_content").html("<div id='size-chart-error'><p class='error-text'>对不起，由于暂时行原因，目前尺码对照表无法显示。</p><p><a href='" + url + "'>请再试一遍</a></p></div>");

                                popover.find("#size-chart-error a").click(function() {
                                    popover.find(".ap_content").html(spinnerContent);
                                    fetchAjax();
                                    return false;
                                });
                            };

                            fetchAjax();
                        });
                    }
                });

                return false;
            };

            return { open : open };
        }();
    </script>

<script type="text/javascript">


  function ajaxUpdate(stateIdx,cityIdx,districtIdx,ASIN,updateSembu,addressSelectSource){

    var params = [];
    params.push("stateIndex=" + encodeURIComponent(stateIdx));
    params.push("cityIndex=" + encodeURIComponent(cityIdx));
    params.push("districtIndex=" + encodeURIComponent(districtIdx));
    params.push("ASIN=" + ASIN);
    params.push("rd=" + Math.random());
    params.push("token=" + encodeURIComponent(jQuery("#ddmToken").text()));
    params.push("updateSembu=" + updateSembu);
    params.push("addressSelectSource=" + addressSelectSource);
    
    jQuery.ajax({
      type: "POST",
      url: "/gp/product/features/dynamic-delivery-message/generate-dynamic-delivery-message.html?ie=UTF8&ie=UTF8",
      contentType: 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded;charset=utf-8',
      data: params.join('&'),
      dataType: "html",
      success: function(objResponse) {
        var resp = objResponse;
        jQuery("#ddmDynamicDisplay").html(resp);
      },
      error: function(xhr) {
        jQuery("#ddmDynamicDisplay").html("对不起，服务器正忙，请稍后再查看配送时间。 ");
      }
    }); // end of jQuery.ajax()
  }

            },

                jQuery("#ddm-destination-address").height(34) ;
                var visibleStrLen = 0;
                jQuery("#ddm-destination-address span").each(function(){
                    if (jQuery(this).css("display") != "none") {
                        visibleStrLen += jQuery(this).text().length;
                    }

                visibleStrLen = (visibleStrLen == 0) ? 20 : visibleStrLen;

                  } else {
                      strLength += 4;
                  }
                  if (cityTriggerText != null && cityTriggerText != ""){
                      strLength += cityTriggerText.length;
                  } else {
                      strLength += 5;
                  }
                  if (districtTriggerText != null && districtTriggerText != ""){
                      strLength += districtTriggerText.length;
                  } else {
                      strLength += 5;
                  }
                  
                  var stateCityDistrictLineWidth = 252 + strLength * 12;

                          }
                      });

                  if (customerAddressLineWidth > stateCityDistrictLineWidth) {
                      ddmPopover.width(customerAddressLineWidth);    
                  } else {
                      ddmPopover.width(stateCityDistrictLineWidth);
                  }
        
                  ddmPopover.click(function(){

                      jQuery("#ddm-shipto-click").css("z-index",popoverZindex);
                  });

        ddmCountDown.getLeftTimeString = function ( remainSeconds ) {
          if (remainSeconds <= 0) return undefined; 
          var remainMins = Math.floor(remainSeconds / 60);
          var minutes = remainMins % 60;
          var hours = Math.floor(remainMins / 60);
          var seconds = remainSeconds % 60;
          var inNext = "内";
          var hourString   =  ( hours == 1 ? "小时" : "小时" );
          var minuteString =  ( minutes  == 1 ? "分钟" : "分钟" );
          var secondString =  ( seconds  == 1 ? "秒" : "秒" );
          if ( hours > 0 && minutes > 0 ){
            return hours + hourString + minutes + minuteString + inNext;
          } else if( hours > 0 && minutes == 0 ){
            return hours + hourString + inNext;
          } else if( hours == 0 && minutes > 0 ){
            return minutes + minuteString + inNext;
          } else if( hours == 0 && minutes == 0 ){
            return seconds + secondString + inNext;
          }

          for( var i = 0; i < this.countdownElementAry.length ; i++){

               });

    window.DPClientLogger = {};
}

window.DPClientLogger.ImpressionLogger = function( program_group, feature, forceUpload) {
    var self = this,
    data = {};

    self.logImpression = function(key) {
      data[key]=1;
      setTimeout( self.upload, 2000 ); // upload client side metrics after 2secs of recording it.  
    };

    self.upload = function() {
      var t = [];
      jQuery.each(data, function(k,v){ t.push(k); });
      data = {};
      if(t.length > 0){
        var protocol = location.protocol == "https:" ? "https://" : "http://",
            url = protocol + ue.furl + "/1/action-impressions/1/OP/" + program_group + "/action/" + feature + ":" + t.join() + "?marketplaceId=" + ue.mid + "&requestId=" + ue.rid + "&session=" + ue.sid + "&_=" + (new Date()).getTime();
        (new Image()).src = url;
      }
    };

    if(forceUpload) {
        jQuery(window).unload(function() { self.upload();});
    }
};
amznJQ.onReady("jQuery", function(){
  amznJQ.declareAvailable("DPClientLogger");
});

});
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
var ma_doc;
var DPCL;

var ma_clicked = 0;
var ma_lastCheck = 0; // timestamp to prevent us messing with the DOM too often
var ma_initCP = 0; // init check pending flag to prevent queueing up of multiple event handler calls
var topCalculatedForNONIE = 0;

var showHideMiniATF = function(isResizeEvent) {
  // Haven't serviced last one yet!
  if(ma_initCP && !isResizeEvent) { return ; }

  // Don't look at the DOM more than once every 400ms
  var lastCheckDiff = new Date().getTime() - ma_lastCheck;
  var checkDelay = (lastCheckDiff < 100 ? 100 - lastCheckDiff : 10);

  ma_initCP = 1;        
  
  var initIfNeeded = function() {
      // show miniATF if Y offset is > 850px else hide it, and show/hide with 200ms delay
      var yPos = ma_doc.scrollTop(), miniATF = jQuery("#gTTLink");
      if( yPos > 650 ){
        
          if( !ma_clicked && miniATF.is(':hidden')){
             miniATF.slideDown(200);
        }
      } else {
        if(miniATF.is(':visible')) 
          miniATF.slideUp(200);
        ma_clicked=0;
      }

      ma_initCP = 0;
      ma_lastCheck = new Date().getTime();
  };

  // Call this function outside of the scroll handler to avoid slowing down scrolling
  setTimeout(initIfNeeded, checkDelay);
};
if(amznJQ) 
 amznJQ.onCompletion('amznJQ.criticalFeature', function() {
  amznJQ.onReady("jQuery", function() {
    ma_doc = jQuery(window);
    jQuery("#gTTLink .ma-back-img").addClass("nav-sprite");
    ma_doc.scroll(function(){showHideMiniATF(0);});
    ma_doc.resize(function(){showHideMiniATF(1);});
    var nonHoverState = function(){
      jQuery("#gTTLink .ma-title").css("color", "#333");
    };
    // go to top on clicking on title with 300ms of scrolling behavior
    jQuery("#gTTLink .maplink, #gTTLink .ma_seeall, #gTTLink .goto-top, #gTTLink .see-all-buying-options").click(function(){ 
      ma_clicked=1;

      if( jQuery(this).hasClass("maplink")){ jQuery(this).attr("href", "javascript:void(0);"); }

      jQuery("#gTTLink").slideUp();
      jQuery("body,html").animate({scrollTop: 0}, 300); 
      nonHoverState();
      return false;
       
    });

    jQuery("#gTTLink .can-add-to-cart").click(function(){ jQuery("#gTTLink .can-add-to-cart a").children().click() } );
    
    // setup on hover experience
    jQuery("#gTTLink .ma-title").hover(function(){ 
      jQuery("#gTTLink .ma-title").css("color", "#E47911");
    }, nonHoverState );
  });
 });
</script>
</div>

</div>

<script type="text/JavaScript">

amznJQ.onReady('JQuery', function() { (function($) {

    window.RECS_rhfShvlLoading = false;
    window.RECS_rhfShvlLoaded = false;
    window.RECS_rhfInView = false;
    window.RECS_rhfMetrics = {};
    $("#rhf_container").show();
    var rhfShvlEventHandler = function () {
        if (   ! window.RECS_rhfShvlLoaded
            && ! window.RECS_rhfShvlLoading
            && $('#rhf_container').size() > 0 ) {
            var yPosition = $(window).scrollTop() + $(window).height();
            var rhfElementFound = $('#rhfMainHeading').size();
            var rhfPosition = $('#rhfMainHeading').offset().top;

            if (/webkit.*mobile/i.test(navigator.userAgent)) {
                rhfPosition -= $(window).scrollTop();
            }

            if (rhfElementFound && ( rhfPosition - yPosition < 400 )) {
                window.RECS_rhfMetrics["start"] = (new Date()).getTime();
                window.RECS_rhfShvlLoading = true;
                var handleSuccess = function (html) {
                    $("#rhf_container").html(html);
                    $("#rhf0Shvl").trigger("render-shoveler");
                    window.RECS_rhfShvlLoaded = true;
                    window.RECS_rhfMetrics["loaded"] = (new Date()).getTime();
                };
                var handleError = function () {
                    $("#rhf_container").hide();
                    $("#rhf_error").show();
                    window.RECS_rhfMetrics["loaded"] = "error";
                };
                $.ajax({
                    url: '/gp/history/external/full-rhf-rec-handler.html',
                    type: "POST",
                    timeout: 10000,
                    data: {
                        shovelerName    : 'rhf0',
                        key             : 'rhf',
                        numToPreload    : '8',
                        isGateway       : 0,
                        refTag          : 'pd_rhf_dp',
                        parentSession   : '479-7800970-2826263',
                        excludeASIN     : 'B009HQ9NUG',
                        renderPopover   : 0,
                        forceSprites    : 1,
                        currentPageType : 'Detail',
                        currentSubPageType : 'Glance',
                        searchAlias     : "",
                        keywords        : "",
                        node            : ""
                    },
                    dataType: "html",
                    success: function (data, status) {
                        handleSuccess(data);
                    },
                    error: function (xhr, status) {
                        handleError();
                    }
                });
            }
        }
    };
    var rhfInView = function() {
        if (!window.RECS_rhfInView && $('#rhf_container').size() > 0) {
            var yPosition = $(window).scrollTop() + $(window).height();
            var rhfElementFound = ($('#rhfMainHeading').size() > 0);
